INNER JOIN (

        SELECT b.Id, b.AdditionalNotes, b.ClientId, b.CreatedAt, b.EndTime, b.ProducerId, b.Purpose, b.RequiresEngineer, b.StartTime, b.Status, b.StudioRoomId, b.TotalPrice, u0.Id, u0.CreatedAt, u0.Email, u0.Name, u0.PhoneNumber, u0.Role, u0.Surname, u0.Address, u0.BillingAddress, u0.CompanyName, u0.Country, u0.DateOfBirth, u0.IsPriorityClient, u0.Notes, u0.Password, u2.Id, u2.CreatedAt, u2.Email, u2.Name, u2.PhoneNumber, u2.Role, u2.Surname, u2.Biography, u2.HourlyRate, u2.IsExternalCollaborator, u2.Specialization, s.Id, s.Capacity, s.EquipmentSummary, s.HasAnalogGear, s.HasVocalBooth, s.HourlyPrice, s.Location, s.Name

            WHERE u.Role == 0

            WHERE u1.Role == 1

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[AdditionalNotes], [b].[ClientId], [b].[CreatedAt], [b].[EndTime], [b].[ProducerId], [b].[Purpose], [b].[RequiresEngineer], [b].[StartTime], [b].[Status], [b].[StudioRoomId], [b].[TotalPrice], [u0].[Id], [u0].[CreatedAt], [u0].[Email], [u0].[Name], [u0].[PhoneNumber], [u0].[Role], [u0].[Surname], [u0].[Address], [u0].[BillingAddress], [u0].[CompanyName], [u0].[Country], [u0].[DateOfBirth], [u0].[IsPriorityClient], [u0].[Notes], [u0].[Password], [u2].[Id], [u2].[CreatedAt], [u2].[Email], [u2].[Name], [u2].[PhoneNumber], [u2].[Role], [u2].[Surname], [u2].[Biography], [u2].[HourlyRate], [u2].[IsExternalCollaborator], [u2].[Specialization], [s].[Id], [s].[Capacity], [s].[EquipmentSummary], [s].[HasAnalogGear], [s].[HasVocalBooth], [s].[HourlyPrice], [s].[Location], [s].[Name]
FROM [Bookings] AS [b]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [u].[Id], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[Email], [u].[Name], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[Role], [u].[Surname], [u].[Address], [u].[BillingAddress], [u].[CompanyName], [u].[Country], [u].[DateOfBirth], [u].[IsPriorityClient], [u].[Notes], [u].[Password]
    FROM [Users] AS [u]
